IDRISS AUTO — CAR IMAGE LIST (cars 1995–now)
========================================

WHERE TO PUT THE IMAGES:  images/cars/
FORMAT:  landscape JPG (16:9, e.g. ~600x340), keep file sizes small (<150 KB ideal).

NAMING RULES (lowercase, exact):
  - Brand image  ->  <brand>.jpg                 e.g.  Audi      -> audi.jpg
  - Model image  ->  <brand>__<model>.jpg        e.g.  Audi A4   -> audi__a4.jpg
    (TWO underscores '__' between brand and model)
  - Model image used if present, else brand image, else a placeholder.
  - You don't need every model — brand images cover the rest.

TOTAL BRANDS: 93   TOTAL MODELS: 4303

########################################
HOW IT WORKS / NEXT STEP
########################################
The app reads images/cars/manifest.json to know which image files exist.
After you drop images into images/cars/, hand them to me and I'll refresh
manifest.json and redeploy (or regenerate it: a JSON array of names without .jpg).
